<p><b>Skitty</b> (<a href="/wiki/List_of_Japanese_Pok%C3%A9mon_names" title="List of Japanese Pokémon names">Japanese</a>: <b>エネコ</b> <i>Eneco</i>) is a <a href="/wiki/Normal_(type)" title="Normal (type)">Normal-type</a> Pokémon.
</p><p>It <a href="/wiki/Evolution" title="Evolution">evolves</a> into <a href="/wiki/Delcatty_(Pok%C3%A9mon)" title="Delcatty (Pokémon)">Delcatty</a> when exposed to a <a href="/wiki/Evolutionary_stone#Moon_Stone" title="Evolutionary stone">Moon Stone</a>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Biology">Biology</span></h2>
<p>Skitty is a pink, feline Pokémon with a stumpy body and four short legs. On its face is a cream-colored, crescent-shaped marking. It has slit-like eyes and tufted ears with purple interiors. Its slender tail has a bulky pink section at the end, terminated by three pin-like structures with yellow ball-like tips. In battle, its tail puffs out, and threatens opponents with a sharp growl.
</p><p>It is fascinated by moving objects, and chases them. It is known to chase its own tail and become dizzy from it. Although it can be difficult to earn its trust, it is very popular due to its adorable looks and behavior. It can use the moves of other Pokémon through the use of <a href="/wiki/Assist_(move)" title="Assist (move)">Assist</a>, its former <a href="/wiki/Signature_move" title="Signature move">signature move</a>. It lives in <a href="/wiki/List_of_Pok%C3%A9mon_by_habitat#Forest_Pok.C3.A9mon" title="List of Pokémon by habitat">holes in trees in forests.</a>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="In_the_anime">In the anime</span></h2>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Skitty_anime.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="http://cdn.bulbagarden.net/upload/thumb/4/4a/Skitty_anime.png/250px-Skitty_anime.png" width="250" height="141" class="thumbimage" srcset="http://cdn.bulbagarden.net/upload/thumb/4/4a/Skitty_anime.png/375px-Skitty_anime.png 1.5x, http://cdn.bulbagarden.net/upload/thumb/4/4a/Skitty_anime.png/500px-Skitty_anime.png 2x" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Skitty_anime.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Skitty in the anime</div></div></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Major_appearances">Major appearances</span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="May.27s_Skitty"><a href="/wiki/May%27s_Skitty" title="May's Skitty">May's Skitty</a></span></h4>
<p>A Skitty appeared <i><a href="/wiki/AG047" title="AG047">I Feel Skitty!</a></i>, where it was caught by <a href="/wiki/May_(anime)" title="May (anime)">May</a>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Other">Other</span></h4>
<p>Skitty's first appearance was in <i><a href="/wiki/SS010" title="SS010">Big Meowth, Little Dreams</a></i>, in which <a href="/wiki/Meowth_(Team_Rocket)" title="Meowth (Team Rocket)">Meowth</a> fell in love with a Skitty.
</p><p>In <i><a href="/wiki/AG060" title="AG060">Delcatty Got Your Tongue</a></i>, May met a former <a href="/wiki/Grand_Festival" title="Grand Festival">Grand Festival</a> winner named <a href="/wiki/Dr._Abby" title="Dr. Abby">Dr. Abby</a> whose Skitty was shown in a flashback.
</p><p>A Skitty appeared in a flashback in <i><a href="/wiki/XY087" title="XY087">A Trip Down Memory Train!</a></i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Minor_appearances">Minor appearances</span></h3>
<p>A Skitty appeared in <i><a href="/wiki/M06" title="M06">Jirachi: Wish Maker</a></i>.
</p><p>A Skitty appeared in <i><a href="/wiki/AG119" title="AG119">The Ribbon Cup Caper</a></i> at the S.S. St. Flower's <a href="/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_Center" title="Pokémon Center">Pokémon Center</a>.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Battle_Frontier_(Hoenn)#Battle_Pike" title="Battle Frontier (Hoenn)" class="mw-redirect">Battle Pike</a> Queen <a href="/wiki/Pike_Queen_Lucy" title="Pike Queen Lucy">Lucy</a> was shown to have a pet Skitty in <i><a href="/wiki/AG158" title="AG158">Queen of the Serpentine</a></i>.
</p><p>A Skitty also appeared in <i><a href="/wiki/DP060" title="DP060">Journey to the Unown!</a></i>
</p><p>A Skitty appeared in <a href="/wiki/Meowth_(Team_Rocket)" title="Meowth (Team Rocket)">Meowth</a>'s fantasy in <i><a href="/wiki/DP117" title="DP117">Noodles: Roamin' Off</a></i>.
</p><p>A <a href="/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_Trainer" title="Pokémon Trainer">Trainer</a>'s Skitty appeared in <i><a href="/wiki/BW103" title="BW103">Curtain Up, Unova League!</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/BW105" title="BW105">Lost at the League!</a></i>.
</p><p>Skitty has made cameo appearances in <i><a href="/wiki/XY001" title="XY001">Kalos, Where Dreams and Adventures Begin!</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/XY002" title="XY002">Lumiose City Pursuit!</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/XY003" title="XY003">A Battle of Aerial Mobility!</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/XY005" title="XY005">A Blustery Santalune Gym Battle!</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/XY009" title="XY009">Clemont's Got a Secret!</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/XY016" title="XY016">A Jolting Switcheroo!</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/XY018" title="XY018">Awakening the Sleeping Giant</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/XY022" title="XY022">Going for the Gold!</a></i>, and <i><a href="/wiki/XY028" title="XY028">The Bonds of Evolution!</a></i>.
</p><p>A <a href="/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_Trainer" title="Pokémon Trainer">Trainer</a>'s Skitty appeared in <i><a href="/wiki/XY026" title="XY026">A Battle by Any Other Name!</a></i>.
</p><p>A <a href="/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_Trainer" title="Pokémon Trainer">Trainer</a>'s Skitty appeared in <i><a href="/wiki/XY039" title="XY039">Summer of Discovery!</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/XY041" title="XY041">Foggy Pokémon Orienteering!</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/XY042" title="XY042">Battling Into the Hall of Fame!</a></i>.
</p><p>Two Skitty appeared in <i><a href="/wiki/XY047" title="XY047">Dreaming a Performer's Dream!</a></i>.
</p><p>A <a href="/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_Trainer" title="Pokémon Trainer">Trainer</a>'s Skitty appeared in <i><a href="/wiki/XY066" title="XY066">Confronting the Darkness!</a></i>.
</p><p>Two Skitty appeared in <i><a href="/wiki/XY090" title="XY090">A Performance Pop Quiz!</a></i>, both under the ownership of unknown <a href="/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_Trainer" title="Pokémon Trainer">Trainers</a>.
</p><p>A <a href="/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_Trainer" title="Pokémon Trainer">Trainer</a>'s Skitty appeared in <a href="/wiki/XY112" title="XY112">XY112</a>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="In_the_manga">In the manga</span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Kiki_Skitty.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="http://cdn.bulbagarden.net/upload/thumb/2/24/Kiki_Skitty.png/300px-Kiki_Skitty.png" width="300" height="232" class="thumbimage" srcset="http://cdn.bulbagarden.net/upload/2/24/Kiki_Skitty.png 1.5x, http://cdn.bulbagarden.net/upload/2/24/Kiki_Skitty.png 2x" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Kiki_Skitty.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Skitty in Pokémon Adventures</div></div></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="In_the_Pok.C3.A9mon_Adventures_manga">In the <a href="/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_Adventures" title="Pokémon Adventures">Pokémon Adventures</a> manga</span></h3>
<dl><dd><i>Main article: <a href="/wiki/Kiki" title="Kiki">Kiki</a></i></dd></dl>
<p>Kiki was one of <a href="/wiki/Ruby_(Adventures)" title="Ruby (Adventures)">Ruby</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Starter_Pok%C3%A9mon" title="Starter Pokémon">first Pokémon</a> along with <a href="/wiki/Nana" title="Nana">Nana</a> and Rara. She is used in the <a href="/wiki/Cute_(condition)" title="Cute (condition)">Cute</a> category of <a href="/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_Contest" title="Pokémon Contest">Pokémon Contests</a> and, like the rest of <a href="/wiki/Category:Ruby%27s_Pok%C3%A9mon" title="Category:Ruby's Pokémon">his Pokémon</a>, is a really powerful <a href="/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_battle" title="Pokémon battle">battler</a>. She evolved into a Delcatty after accidentally being exposed to a Moon Stone on <a href="/wiki/Steven_Stone" title="Steven Stone">Steven Stone</a>'s belt.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Shauna" title="Shauna">Shauna</a> owns a Skitty in the <a href="/wiki/X_%26_Y_chapter_(Adventures)" title="X &amp; Y chapter (Adventures)"><i>X &amp; Y</i> chapter</a>.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="In_the_TCG">In the TCG</span></h2>
<dl><dd><i>Main article: <a href="/wiki/Skitty_(TCG)" title="Skitty (TCG)">Skitty (TCG)</a></i></dd></dl>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Game_data">Game data</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="NPC_appearances">NPC appearances</span></h3>
<ul><li> <a href="/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_Ranger_(game)" title="Pokémon Ranger (game)">Pokémon Ranger</a>: Teresa, a resident of <a href="/wiki/Fall_City" title="Fall City">Fall City</a>, owns six Skitty. When they all run away during the second numbered mission, she gets the player to retrieve them for her.</li></ul>

<td class="roundy" style="vertical-align: middle; border: 1px solid #9DC1B7; padding-left:3px;"> It can't stop itself from chasing moving things, and it runs in a circle, chasing its own tail.
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="roundy" style="width: 80px; max-width: 80px; background:#EA1A3E; border: 2px solid #EA1A3E; line-height:12pt;"> <a href="/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_Y" title="Pokémon Y" class="mw-redirect"><span style="color:#000;">Y </span></a>
</th>
<td class="roundy" style="vertical-align: middle; border: 1px solid #9DC1B7; padding-left:3px;"> It shows its cute side by chasing its own tail until it gets dizzy.
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="roundy" style="width: 80px; max-width: 80px; background:#AB2813; border: 2px solid #AB2813; line-height:12pt;"> <a href="/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_Omega_Ruby" title="Pokémon Omega Ruby" class="mw-redirect"><span style="color:#FFF;">Omega Ruby </span></a>
</th>
<td class="roundy" style="vertical-align: middle; border: 1px solid #9DC1B7; padding-left:3px;"> Skitty has the habit of becoming fascinated by moving objects and chasing them around. This Pokémon is known to chase after its own tail and become dizzy.
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="roundy" style="width: 80px; max-width: 80px; background:#26649C; border: 2px solid #26649C; line-height:12pt;"> <a href="/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_Alpha_Sapphire" title="Pokémon Alpha Sapphire" class="mw-redirect"><span style="color:#FFF;">Alpha Sapphire </span></a>
</th>
<td class="roundy" style="vertical-align: middle; border: 1px solid #9DC1B7; padding-left:3px;"> Skitty is known to chase around playfully after its own tail. In the wild, this Pokémon lives in holes in the trees of forests. It is very popular as a pet because of its adorable looks.
</td></tr></table>
</td></tr></table>
</td></tr></table><br style="clear:both;" />

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Learnset">Learnset</span></h3>
<p>All moves that do damage that do not normally have STAB will have STAB if Skitty has the Ability <a href="/wiki/Normalize_(Ability)" title="Normalize (Ability)">Normalize</a>.

<ul><li>Moves marked with an asterisk (*) must be <a href="/wiki/Chain_breeding" title="Chain breeding"><span style="color:#000;">chain bred</span></a> onto Skitty in Generation VI</li>
<li>Moves marked with a double dagger (‡) can only be bred from a Pokémon who learned the move in an earlier generation.</li>
<li>Moves marked with a superscript game abbreviation can only be bred onto Skitty in that game.</li>
<li><b>Bold</b> indicates a move that gets <a href="/wiki/Same-type_attack_bonus" title="Same-type attack bonus"><span style="color:#000;">STAB</span></a> when used by Skitty</li>
<li><i>Italic</i> indicates a move that gets STAB only when used by an evolution  of Skitty</li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Evolution">Evolution</span></h3>
<table style="margin:auto; text-align:center; background: #A8A878; border-radius: 10px; -moz-border-radius: 10px; -webkit-border-radius: 10px; -khtml-border-radius: 10px; -icab-border-radius: 10px; -o-border-radius: 10px; border: 3px solid #6D6D4E;">

<tr>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span></h2>
<ul><li> Because of its inclusion in the <a href="/wiki/Field_(Egg_Group)" title="Field (Egg Group)">Field Egg Group</a>, it is possible to breed two Pokémon as different as Skitty and <a href="/wiki/Wailord_(Pok%C3%A9mon)" title="Wailord (Pokémon)">Wailord</a> together. This has become the center of the <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Fan_terminology#HSOWA" title="Appendix:Fan terminology">Hot Skitty on Wailord Action</a> joke.</li>
<li> The cream-colored section of Skitty's face is shaped like a crescent moon, which may be related to the fact that Skitty evolves using a <a href="/wiki/Evolutionary_stone#Moon_Stone" title="Evolutionary stone">Moon Stone</a>.</li>
<li> Prior to <a href="/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_Platinum_Version" title="Pokémon Platinum Version">Platinum</a>, a Skitty with <a href="/wiki/Normalize_(Ability)" title="Normalize (Ability)">Normalize</a> could not directly damage a <a href="/wiki/Ghost_(type)" title="Ghost (type)">Ghost-type</a> Pokémon. It now can, however, by learning <a href="/wiki/Foresight_(move)" title="Foresight (move)">Foresight</a>.</li>
<li> The <a href="/wiki/Escape_item#Fluffy_Tail" title="Escape item">Fluffy Tail</a>, an item that allows escape from battle in the same way that a <a href="/wiki/Escape_item#Pok.C3.A9_Doll" title="Escape item">Poké Doll</a> does, resembles Skitty's tail. It was likely introduced because <a href="/wiki/Clefairy_(Pok%C3%A9mon)" title="Clefairy (Pokémon)">Clefairy</a> cannot be found in <a href="/wiki/Hoenn" title="Hoenn">Hoenn</a>.</li>
<li>Skitty is the only Generation III Pokémon that evolves via <a href="/wiki/Evolutionary_stone#Moon_Stone" title="Evolutionary stone">Moon Stone</a>.</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Origin">Origin</span></h3>
<p>Skitty is based on a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/kitten" class="extiw" title="wp:kitten">kitten</a> with its tail resembling <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Foxtail_(diaspore)" class="extiw" title="wp:Foxtail (diaspore)">foxtail grass</a>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Name_origin">Name origin</span></h4>
<p>Skitty is a combination of <i>skittish</i> and <i>kitty</i> (slang for <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/cat" class="extiw" title="wp:cat">cat</a></i>).
</p><p>Eneco is a combination of 狗尾草 <i>enokorogusa</i> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Foxtail_(diaspore)" class="extiw" title="wp:Foxtail (diaspore)">foxtail grass</a>, a type of plant that Skitty's tail resembles) and 猫 <i>neko</i> (cat).
</p>
